$(function(){
		$('.newBtnKcSearch').click(function(){
		var exam_type = $('#ksLeiing').attr("value");
		var exam_gradation = $('#ksJied').attr("value");
		var zone_code = $('#kcShenf').attr("value");
		var give_type = $('#kcLeixing').attr("value");
		var url = 'http://kc.offcn.com/c_'+give_type+'_'+exam_type+'_'+exam_gradation+'_'+zone_code+'_.html'
		//window.location.href = url;
		$(".newBtnKcSearch").attr("href",url);

	});
});
